Working with NCD
Creating NCD Files from FWL Files
NCD files are created from a list of FWL-files to be specified as a list in a configuration file.
The location for the generated NCD files is also set in this configuration file.
In addition, it contains the specification of a VIN, which is required to calculate the CPS (Coding
Proof Stamp) of the NCD files.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -fwl2ncd <config file> (deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -fwl2Ncd <config file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -fwl2ncd <config file> (deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -server -fwl2Ncd <config file>
Declaration:
-fwl2Ncd <config file> Absolute path to configuration file.
<config file>…Absolute path to configuration file
Example:
226
E-Sys.bat -fwl2Ncd C:\conf\fwl.properties
Information:
The <config file> must contain the following entries:
# Absolute path of an FA file. E.g. FA = C:/Data/fa.xml
FA = <FA file>
# e.g. NCD_DIR = C:/NCD
NCD_DIR = <NCD destination folder>
# e.g. FWL_LIST = C:/FWL/flw_1.fwl;C:/FWL/flw_2.fwl;
FWL_LIST = <path to fwl1>; <path to fwl2>;
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Reading of Netto Coding Data
The Netto Coding Data of the ECUs is read out for all CAFs present in the SVT and stored as FWL and
NCD files.
In addition, the VIN is determined and used to determine the file name.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readncd <SVT> -connection <config file> -out <NCD-directory> (deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -readNcd <SVT file> -connection <config file> -out <NCD directory> [-
notReadVin]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readncd <SVT> -connection <config file> -out <NCD-directory>
(deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -server -readNcd <SVT file> -connection <config file> -out <NCD directory>
[-notReadVin]
227
Declaration:
-readNcd <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-out <NCD directory> Absolute path to output-directory.
-notReadVin VIN is not read from the Master ECU if used
Example:
E-Sys.bat -readNcd C:\Data\SVT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -out
C:\Data\CAF
Information:
• The file name of the FWL file is formed according to the following pattern:
"<VIN>_<CAF>_<BV>.fwl".
◦ VIN: the last 7 digits of the VIN from the VIN-Master
◦ CAF: SGBM-number of the CAF used
◦ BV: Name of the basic variant
• The file name of the NCD-file is formed according to the following pattern: "<SGBMID>.caf.<MV>
<SV><PV>.ncd"
◦ SGBMID: SGBM-ID of the CAF used
◦ MV: Main version of the CAF used
◦ SV: Sub version of the CAF used
◦ PV: Patch version of the CAF used
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Signing of Netto Coding Data
This command signs a list of NCD-files for the corresponding boot loaders..
The NCDs must be complete (incl. CPS). Validation or modification of the NCD-files is no longer
possible after the signature.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -ncdsign <config file> (deprecated)
228
E-Sys.bat -signNcd <config file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -ncdsign <config file> (deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -server -signNcd <config file>
Declaration:
-signNcd <config file> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -server -signNcd C:\NCD\ncdSign.config
Information:
• In client-mode, the command is supported only in combination with Certificate-basedauthentication.
• In server-client-mode, the user must first log in to the backend using the -authenticationCoding
command.
• Required parameters are FA and NCD_LIST_1.
• Optional parameters are BACKEND_SIGNATURE, SHIPMENT_NCD_GENERATION,
SIGNED_NCD_DIR, and SHIPMENT_NCD_DIR. If omitted, the information from the ESys.properties-file is read or default settings are used.
• Depending on the BACKEND_SIGNATURE-setting (ALLOW - allow, MUST_NOT - prohibit, FORCE -
enforce) the NCDs are signed in the backend or local.
• The SHIPMENT_NCD_GENERATION-setting controls the calculation and signing of NCDs for
delivery status. If omitted, NCDs for delivery status are then calculated and signed.
• If multiple NCD lists are defined, the NCD_LIST_x-key must be unique.
• If multiple NCD lists are defined, the bootloader-number <BTLD-Nummer-x> must be unique.
• A '\' may not be used in the configuration file. Instead, use '/' or '\\' for path information.
The format of the configuration file to pass is defined as follows:
# Absolute path of an FA file. E.g. FA = C:/Data/fa.xml
FA = <FA file>
# Format MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW
BACKEND_SIGNATURE = <MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW>
229
# Generate shipment NCDs. DEFAULT = on
# Format: on | off
SHIPMENT_NCD_GENERATION = <on|off>
# z.B. SIGNED_NCD_DIR = C:/NCD/signed
SIGNED_NCD_DIR = <Destination directory for signed NCD>
# z.B. SHIPMENT_NCD_DIR = C:/NCD/shipment
SHIPMENT_NCD_DIR = <Destination directory for signed NCD>
# Format <BTLD-Number>;<NCD-Pfad> , z.B.
"00001234;C:/NCD/CAFD_0000DDDD_026_000_002.ncd;C:/NCD/CAFD_0000BBBB_006_011_008.ncd"
NCD_LIST_1 = <BTLD-Nummer-1>;<NCD-1>;<NCD-2>;<NCD-3>;<NCD-4>
# Optional parameter
# If specified, only client-batch-mode is considered
# Default value = off
USE_SWL_SEC_CERTIFICATE = <on|off>
# Optional parameter.
# Considered only in client-batch-mode
# If the parameter is owithted SWL_SEC_CONNECTION, the value from `Esys.properties` is
used.
SWL_SEC_CONNECTION = <bmw_intranet|internet>
Example for a configuration file:
# Absolute path of an FA file. E.g. FA = C:/Data/fa.xml
FA = <FA file>
# Format MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW
BACKEND_SIGNATURE = ALLOW
# Generate shipment NCDs. DEFAULT = on
# Format: on | off
SHIPMENT_NCD_GENERATION = off
# z.B. SIGNED_NCD_DIR = C:/NCDs/signed
SIGNED_NCD_DIR = C:/NCD/signed
# z.B. SHIPMENT_NCD_DIR = C:/NCD/shipment
SHIPMENT_NCD_DIR = C:/NCD/shipment
# Format <BTLD-Nummer>;<NCD path>
NCD_LIST_1 =
00001ffd;C:/NCD/CAFD_0000AAAA_006_011_017.ncd;C:/NCD/CAFD_0000BBBB_006_011_008.ncd;
NCD_LIST_2 =
00001c44;C:/NCD/CAFD_0000CCCC_026_000_000.ncd;C:/NCD/CAFD_0000DDDD_026_000_002.ncd;
230
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Calculate Netto Coding Data (NCD)
Similar to the GUI module coding verification, a verification can be performed in batch mode after
specifying a vehicle order (FA) and thus Netto Coding Data (NCD) can be calculated.
During verification, NCD- and FP-traces as well as a verification report are generated and stored in
the trace-directory.
Verification is performed on all FAs at the FA-list and all imported CAFs.
The optional parameter [-caf] allows verification to be restricted to individual (imported) CAFs.
If multiple CAFs are specified, the names are separated by commas (",").
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -generatencd <FA file> [-caf <CAF name>] -trace <trace directory>
(deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -generateNcd <FA file> [-caf <CAF name>] -trace <trace directory>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -generatencd <FA file> [-caf <CAF name>] -trace <trace directory>
(deprecated)
E-Sys.bat -server -generateNcd <FA file> [-caf <CAF name>] -trace <trace directory>
Declaration:
-generateNcd <FA file> Absolute path of an FA- or FA-list-file.
-caf <CAF name> Name of the CAF to be verified.
-trace <trace directory> Absolute path of the directory to which the data
to be generated is to be written.
Example:
E-Sys.bat-generateNcd C:\Data\FA\F020.xml -trace C:\Data\Trace -caf
231
cafd_0000815.caf.001_001_003
Information:
• No check will be performed to verify that the trace directory is empty. This means that existing
files in the trace directory can be overwritten without warning.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Calculate NCD-Testdata
NCD test data will be created and signed based on a list of CAF files, which have to be specified in a
configuration file.
In addition to the CAFs, a vehicle order (file name + absolute path) must be specified in the
configuration file.
It is also mandatory to provide a BTLD SGBM number, as this is required for signing the NCDs.
Optionally, the storage location for the generated NCD files can also be specified in the
configuration file.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -generateTestNcds <config file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -generateTestNcds <config file>
Declaration:
-generateTestNcds <configuration file> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -generateTestNcds C:\conf\MyConfigForTestdata.cfg
Information:
232
• In client mode, the command is only supported in combination with Certificate-based
authentication.
• In client-server mode, the user must first log in with a separate command to the backend.
• If the BACKEND_SIGNATURE parameter is omitted, the value from Esys.properties is used.
• If the parameter NCD_TEST_DATA_DIR is omitted, then the E-Sys data directory is read from
Esys.properties and from this a path is constructed to the folder in which the target folder "NCD
test data" is created.
• Generation of test NCDs for Coding 2:
• FA file must contain exactly 1 FA
• Generation of test NCDs for Coding 3:
• FA file must contain exactly 2 FAs
• FAs must include Test-VINs (11. char of Long-VIN is 'H')
• FAs must not be identical, i.e. they must differ in at least one of the following points: colour
code, fabric code, time criteria, SA entries, E entries, K entries
The format of the configuration file is defined as follows:
# e.g. FA = C:/FA/fa_I020.xml
FA = <Vehicle order with absolute path>
# e.g. BTLD = 00001234
BTLD = <BTLD SGBM-Number>
# e.g. CAF_LIST = "cafd_0000DDDD.caf.026_000_002;cafd_0000BBBB.caf.006_011_008"
CAF_LIST = <CAF_file_name_1>;<CAF_file_name_2>;<CAF_file_name_3>;..
# Optional parameter
# e.g. NCD_TEST_DATA_DIR = C:/Testdata
NCD_TEST_DATA_DIR = <target folder for the ZIP-file containing the NCD-Testdata>
# Optional parameter
# Format MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW
BACKEND_SIGNATURE = <MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW>
# Optional parameter. Will be only considered in the Client Batch-Mode.
# If the parameter SWL_SEC_CONNECTION is missing, the value from `Esys.properties`
will be used instead.
SWL_SEC_CONNECTION = <bmw_intranet|internet>
At the end of the execution a generation report will be created. After the NCD-Calculation this
report file will be placed in parallel to the generated ZIP-Archive.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
233
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Netto Coding Data (NCD) for customer vehicles
Similar to the GUI module 'NCD-Preparation', it is also possible to request NCDs in the SCB backend
in batch mode.
For this process, a list of vehicle orders (FA_LIST) is required, which must contain at least one entry.
In addition to the FA_LIST, either SVT or TAL must be defined.
The generated NCD files are stored in a directory after the command has been executed. This
storage location can also be defined in the configuration file if required (SIGNED_NCD_DIR).
If the specification of an alternative storage location is missing, then the default directory for
signed NCDs from Esys.properties is used.
This command can be used only in the BMW environment, because there is a communication with
the Secure Coding Backend (SCB).
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -createCustomerNcd <config file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -createCustomerNcd <config file>
Declaration:
-createCustomerNcd <configuration file> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -createCustomerNcd C:\conf\configForSCB.cfg
Information:
• The calculation and signing of the NCDs will be done in the SCB backend
• As a necessary precondition for the access to the SCB backend, a TIS-client Certificate has to be
imported first
• The URLs used for connecting to the SCB have to be defined in the Esys.properties file by using
the property key scb.backend.url
• Required parameters are FA_LIST and either SVT or TAL.
234
• The configuration file can contain either an SVT or a TAL, but not both.
• Optional parameter is SIGNED_NCD_DIR. If omitted, the information from the E-Sys.propertiesfile is read or default settings are used.
The format of the configuration file is defined as follows:
# e.g. FA_LIST = C:/Data/FA/fa_1.xml;C:/Data/FA/fa_2.xml;
FA_LIST = <Absolute path FA1>;<Absolute path FA2>;<Absolute path FA3>
# e.g. SVT = C:/Data/SVT/svt.xml
SVT = <Absolute path SVT>
# e.g. TAL = C:/Data/SVT/tal.xml
TAL = <Absolute path TAL>
# Optional parameter.
# e.g. SIGNED_NCD_DIR = C:/Data/NCD
SIGNED_NCD_DIR = <target folder for the NCD data>
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
NCD preparation from SVT
Similar to the GUI module 'NCD-Preparation', it is also possible to calculate and sign NCDs taking
into account the CAFDs present on a given SVT file.
For this process, a list of vehicle orders (FA) is required, which must contain at least one entry.
In addition to the FA, a SVT must also be defined.
The generated NCD files are stored in the signed and default NCD folders specified by
Esys.properties.
If local signing is not possible, then a communication with the Secure Coding Backend (SCB) is
needed. Should that happen, authentication is required. More information about it, including
particularities of client-server vs client only operation, can be found here.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -generateNcdFromSvt <configuration file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
235
E-Sys.bat -server -generateNcdFromSvt <configuration file>
Declaration:
-generateNcdFromSvt <configuration file> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -generateNcdFromSvt C:\conf\config.cfg
Information:
• As a necessary precondition for the access to the SCB backend, a TIS-client Certificate has to be
imported first
• The URLs used for connecting to the SCB have to be defined in the Esys.properties file by using
the property key scb.backend.url
• Required parameters are FA and SVT.
• Optional parameter is BACKEND_SIGNATURE. If omitted, the information from the ESys.properties-file is read or default settings are used.
The format of the configuration file is defined as follows:
# e.g. FA = C:/FA/fa_I020.xml
FA = <Absolute path FA>
# e.g. SVT = C:/Data/SVT/svt.xml
SVT = <Absolute path SVT>
# Optional parameter
# If the parameter BACKEND_SIGNATURE is missing, the value from `Esys.properties` will
be used instead.
# Format MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW
BACKEND_SIGNATURE = <MUST_NOT | FORCE | ALLOW>
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
20.5. CVN / OBD
CVNs (Calibration Verification Number) are calculated via the OBD-relevant (On-Board Diagnostics)
SWEn for a control unit and compared with the CVNs that are read from the ECUs. 
The ECUs and SWEs required for the calculation are read from an SVT document. 
The CVN values and the comparison results are written to a report file as text or in XML format (
236
-xmlreport). 
The SVT document can be read from the ECU, from the VCM, or from a file to be specified.
Legend:
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
Calculate CVN
The following command can be used to calculate CVN values.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -cvncalculation <FA file> -out <OBD-CVN-FA-List file> [-caf <CAF name>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -cvncalculation <FA file> -out <OBD-CVN-FA-List file> [-caf <CAF
name>]
Declaration:
-cvncalculation <FA file> Absolute path of an FA- or FA-list-file.
-out <OBD-CVN-FA-List file> Absolute path of the output-file.
-caf <CAF name> Names of the CAFs to use.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -cvncalculation C:\Data_3_39_1_09f71b0_64bit_JDK11\FA\FaListSample.xml -out
C:\Data_3_39_1_09f71b0_64bit_JDK11\Etc\CVN.xml -caf cafd_000000ae.caf.001_002_003
Information:
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Compare CVN
Command in client batch mode:
237
E-Sys.bat -comparecvn -connection <config file> [-sg <ecu list>] (-svt <SVT
file>\|-svtvcmist\|-svtvcmsoll\|-svtecu) -trace <trace directory> [-fa <FA file>] [
-xmlreport]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -comparecvn -connection <config file> [-sg <ecu list>] (-svt <SVT
file>\|-svtvcmist\|-svtvcmsoll\|-svtecu) -trace <trace directory> [-fa <FA file>] [
-xmlreport]
Declaration:
-comparecvn command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-sg <ecu list> ECU-filters. If the parameter is specified, only
ECUs from the list are processed. The ECUs are
separated by commas in the list.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
-svtvcmist The SVTist is read from the VCM.
-svtvcmsoll The SVTsoll is read from the VCM.
-svtecu The SVT is read from the ECU.
-trace <trace directory> Absolute path to the directory for the report-file.
-fa <FA file> Absolute path to the FA-List-file. If the parameter
"-fa" is not specified, the FA is read out of the
vehicle.
-xmlreport Create a report-file im XML-Format.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -comparecvn -trace C:\Data\trace -svtecu -fa C:\Data\FA\FaList.xml -sg
ZBE,ZGW -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
Information:
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
238
20.6. Read data

• () selection, must be specified

Read BRV:

console.

Command in client-server batch mode:
239

Serie.
Example:

Information:
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Read FA:
The vehicle-order is read out of the vehicle and stored in a file.
If only one directory is specified, the VIN is also determined and used to determine the file-name.
Otherwise, the specified file will be used. If it already exists, it will be overwritten.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readfa -connection <config file> -out <FA directory>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readfa -connection <config file> -out <FA directory>
Declaration:
-readfa command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
240
-out <FA directory> Absolute path for the output directory with or
without file-specification.
Example:
E-Sys.bat-readfa -out C:\Data\FA -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
E-Sys.bat-readfa -out C:\Data\FA\FA_123.xml -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
Information:
• If no file-name is specified, it is determined after the pattern "FA_<VIN>_<Timestamp>.xml".
◦ VIN………………. the last 7 digits of the VIN from the VIN-Master
◦ Timestamp…….. Timestamp according to the pattern ddmmyyyyhhmm
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Read SVT:
The SVT is read by the vehicle and stored in a file.
If only one directory is specified, the VIN is also determined and used to determine the file-name.
Otherwise, the specified file will be used. If it already exists, it will be overwritten.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readsvt -connection <config file> -out <SVT directory>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readsvt -connection <config file> -out <SVT directory>
Declaration:
-readsvt command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-out <SVT directory> Absolute path for the output directory with or
without file specification.
241
Example:
E-Sys.bat -readsvt -out C:\Data\SVT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
E-Sys.bat -readsvt -out C:\Data\SVT\SVT_123.xml -connection C:\conf
\connection.properties
Information:
• If no file-name is specified, it is determined after the pattern "SVT_<VIN>_<Timestamp>.xml".
◦ VIN………………. the last 7 digits of the VIN from the VIN-Master
◦ Timestamp…….. Timestamp according to the pattern ddmmyyyyhhmm
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Read SVT with Smart Actuators:
The SVT is read by the vehicle and stored in a file. Also adds SmAc information to the file.
If only one directory is specified, the VIN is also determined and used to determine the file-name.
Otherwise, the specified file will be used. If it already exists, it will be overwritten.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readsvtsmac -connection <config file> -out <SVT directory>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readsvtsmac -connection <config file> -out <SVT directory>
Declaration:
-readsvtsmac command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-out <SVT directory> Absolute path for the output directory with or
without file specification.
Example:
242
E-Sys.bat -readsvtsmac -out C:\Data\SVT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
E-Sys.bat -readsvtsmac -out C:\Data\SVT\SVT_123.xml -connection C:\conf
\connection.properties
Information:
• If no file-name is specified, it is determined after the pattern "SVT_<VIN>_<Timestamp>.xml".
◦ VIN………………. the last 7 digits of the VIN from the VIN-Master
◦ Timestamp…….. Timestamp according to the pattern ddmmyyyyhhmm
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
List available projects:
This command lists the available projects that were previously imported. Information on how to
import projects can be found at PDX Containers.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -projects [series separated by commas]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -projects [series separated by commas]
Declaration:
-projects command.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -projects
E-Sys.bat -projects F001
E-Sys.bat -projects F001,G070
Information:
• If no series is specified, all available projects will be listed on the console. To filter a series,
243
specify it after the command. To filter several series, separate them with commas.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.
◦ 2 - None of the available projects matched the provided filters.
◦ 4 - No projects were found.

Update SVT from PDX container
With this command, the SVT will be updated with SWE versions existing in the container.
 The most recent version of the SWE found in the PDX container will be considered.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -updateSvt -svt <SVT file> -pdx <PDX container> [-out] <SVT file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat - server -updateSvt -svt <SVT file> -pdx <PDX container> [-out] <SVT file>
Declaration:
-updateSvt Command.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
-pdx <PDX container> Absolute path to PDX container
-out Optional parameter. Absolute path to alternative
SVT-file
Example:
E-Sys.bat -updateSvt -svt "C:\Data\SVT\SVT_target.xml" -pdx "C:\Data\ODX
\G045_25_07_420_Q.066_007_031.pdx"
244
E-Sys.bat -updateSvt -svt "C:\Data\SVT\SVT_target.xml" -pdx "C:\Data\ODX
\G045_25_07_420_Q.066_007_031.pdx" -out "SVT_updated.xml"
Information:
• Each updated SWE will be printed in the console
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.

parameter).

-engineering Argument.
-vin <VIN17> 17-digit VIN.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to The SVT-file.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.

◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.

-diagaddress <diagnosis address>\|`-svt <SVT file>`)
Declaration:
-clearSecureToken command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-featureid <FeatureID> FeatureID in Hex, e.g. 0x23.
-diagaddress <diagnosis address> Diagnostic address of the ECU in hex.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
Information:
• All ECUs must be in engineering mode.
• The following codes are returned:
256
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.

Activate/Deactivate SecOC
The SecOC Activate and Deactivate commands update the Security Onboard Communication
(SecOC) for a specified group of Electronic Control Units (ECUs). Moreover, it provides the capability
to update and reset all ECUs following the update.
268
Activate SecOC
Action to comfortably enable the SecOC Lcs and update the ServicePack Lcs according to each ECU
Service Pack (SP) and the SP of the SecOC Master Boardnet.

-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]

parameter.)

LCS.

-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.

Activate/Deactivate/Read ACL
SP25 introduced ACL (access control list). The ACL allows defined SOME/IP communiction in a form
of a whitelist. ACL protection can be started or stopped and the current ACL status can be read out.
The control units are delivered with an inactive ACL.
Activate ACL
Action to activate the ACL in an ECU or list of ECUs.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -activateAcl -connection <config file> -svt <SVT file> [-blacklist <file>] [
-whitelist <file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -activateAcl -connection <config file> -svt <SVT file> [-blacklist
<file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Declaration:
-activateAcl Command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter.)
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file. (Optional)
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file. (Optional)
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
270
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.

20.9. Server-client batch mode
Legend:
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
Start E-Sys-Batch-Server
Command to start an E-Sys-Batch-Server.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -startserver
or
E-Sys.bat –startserver [-prop <property file>]
  [-setProxy <configuration file> ]
  [-authenticationCoding ( -user <username> | -useSwlSecCertificate )
-connection
<bmw_intranet|internet>]
  [-authenticationSfa]
Command in client-server batch mode:
---Only applicable in client-operation---
Declaration:
-startserver Command to start the server
-prop <property file> Absolute path to the E-Sys-property-file to be
used.
-setProxy <config file> Absolute path to Proxy-Configuration-file.
-authenticationCoding Argument.
273
-user <username> Secure Coding: Backend-Login via username
(BASIC). Example: max.mustermann).
-useSwlSecCertificate Secure Coding: Backend-Login via Certificate
(CERTIFICATE).
-connection <bmw_intranet|internet> Secure Coding: Login via bmw_intranet (inside
BMW-network) or internet (outside BMWnetwork).
-authenticationSfa Argument.
-dialog Backend-Login with GUI-dialog.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -startserver
E-Sys.bat –startserver -prop C:\config\Esys.properties -authenticationCoding -user
max.mustermann -connection intranet -dialog
E-Sys.bat –startserver -prop C:\config\Esys.properties -setProxy C:\data
\proxyConfig.config
-authenticationCoding -useSwlSecCertificate -connection internet
E-Sys.bat –startserver -prop C:\config\Esys.properties -setProxy C:\data
\proxyConfig.config
-authenticationCoding -useSwlSecCertificate -connection internet -authenticationSfa
E-Sys.bat –startserver -authenticationSfa
Information:
• If the parameter -authenticationCoding is set, the E-Sys server is only started if the SWL-Sec2 is
successfully authenticated. See the details of the parameter below.
• If the parameter -setProxy is set, the E-Sys-server is only started if SWL-Sec2 can be reached via
the proxy-server. For details on the parameter, see Proxy
• If the parameter -authenticationSfa is set. The client certificate that is still required must have
already been imported. This is only done with the respective backend request.
• If the switch -dialog is included, a GUI-dialog is displayed in which login data must be entered.
• It makes no sense to specify the property-file (-prop <property file>) in connection with a
client-request to the server (-server) because the property-file is not used by the server. The
server uses the property-file loaded at server-startup.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - Errors occurred so that the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
274
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.

Check if an E-Sys-Batch-Server is active
Command to check if an E-Sys-Batch-Server has been started.
Command in client batch mode:
---Only applicable in server-client-operation---
Command in client-server batch mode:

E-Sys.bat –server –closeconnection
E-Sys.bat –server -stop
20.10. FA convert
It converts OrderXML-files (vehicle order) from a specified path to FA (vehicle-order-files). 
The file-names of the OrderXML-files must correspond to pattern A<xxxxxxx>.xml (x = letter or
digit).
Legend:
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
278
Convert OrderXML to FA
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -convertorderxml <FO directory> -out <FA directory>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -convertorderxml <FO directory> -out <FA directory>
Declaration:
-convertorderxml <FO directory> Absolute path to the directory with the FO files.
-out <FA directory> Absolute path to the directory for the storage of
the FA files.
Example:
E-Sys.bat-convertorderxmlc:\Data\FO-outC:\Data\FA
Information:
• For each OrderXML-file, an FA-file is created with the file-name pattern
"<OrderXML>_FA_<Timestamp>.xml".
◦ OrderXML………… Name of OrderXML
◦ Timestamp………. Time stamp according to the pattern ddmmyyyyhhmm
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred, so no verification was possible.
◦ 2 - Errors have occurred while processing individual files. It is possible that individual files
have been converted correctly.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.

Batch-command for executeFv

Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -executeFv <config file> [-ignoreBATHAF]
Declaration:
-executeFv <config file> Absolute path to executeFv-Configuration-file.

Example:
E-Sys.bat -executeFv C:\data\executeFV.config -ignoreBATHAF
Information:
Information: about the batch-command -executeFv can be obtained from the "executeFv manual".
• If a BAT/HAF test reveals that switch S1 is open, the further execution of the command depends
on parameter -ignoreBATHAF.
◦ -ignoreBATHAF has been set: The flash sequence continues. However, the user must be aware
that the execution can lead to interruptions. In this case, the TAL-processing cannot be
ended with value 0 (OK), but at best with value 4 (with warning).
◦ -ignoreBATHAF not set: The execution of the command -talexecution is canceled.
• An eight hexadecimal character code is returned with the format:
[Overall] [Not defined] [ErrorLcs] [ErrorIPSec] [ErrorEcuModes] [ErrorCert] [ErrorTal]
[ErrorVcm]
Possible values:
• 0: Success
• 1: Error
• 2: Warning
• 3: not processed
• F: not defined
Example: 1F021333

20.12. PDX Containers
Legend:
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
PDX-Import
This command can be used to import containers (KC, IC or PDX template) into the programming
system.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -pdximport <PDX container file> -project <project name>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -pdximport <PDX container file> -project <project name>
Declaration:
-pdximport <PDX container file> Absolute path of the container to be imported.
-project <project name> Name of the project to import a container into.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -pdximport C:\Data\ODX\TEST__03__I020.001_023_015.pdx -project
TEST__03__I020_001_023_015
Important additional information for partial KCs:
If you want to import a constructed container (maybe by yourself) you have to keep in mind, that
281
the referenced software unit(s) (SWE) won’t be imported into psdzdata. 
 The referenced SWE(s) are only a reference and do not exist as actual data in the Container, so it is
 not possible to import the actual data.
In case the referenced software unit(s) are going to be needed, they have to imported by an other
container, in which the needed software unit(s) exist as a real data.
Information:
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
PDX-Update
This command can be used to update containers with a PDX-template.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -pdxupdate <PDX container file> [-out <PDX container file>] -template <PDX
template file> [-uncompressedPDX]
[-saveExtractedPDXFolder] [-loadExtractedPDX]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -pdxupdate <PDX container file> [-out <PDX container file>]
-template <PDX template file> [-uncompressedPDX]
[-saveExtractedPDXFolder] [-loadExtractedPDX]
Declaration:
-pdxupdate <PDX container file> Absolute path of the container whose template is
to be updated.
-out <PDX container file> Absolute path of the container to be created. If
the -out parameter is owithted, the container is
saved with the same name after the update.
-template <PDX template file> Absolute path of the PDX-template, which the
container should contain after the update.
-uncompressedPDX Flag indicating whether the PDX file is generated
uncompressed. This might make the generation
faster but the PDX files will also be larger.
282
-saveExtractedPDXFolder Flag indicating where the extracted PDX will be
persisted after E-Sys is closed
-loadExtractedPDX Flag indicating where the extracted PDX
directory will be used to load instead of the PDX
file. It will lead to faster loading
Example:
E-Sys.bat -pdxupdate C:\Data\ODX\TEST__03__I020.001_023_015.pdx -out C:\Data\ODX
\TEST__03__I020.001_023_020.pdx -template C:\Data\ODX\PT01_template.003_040_000.pdx
Information:
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Create PDX-component-containers
This command can be used to create component-containers.
Partial PDX-component-container:
It is also possible to create a partial PDX-component-container. Here, a md5 hash value is used to
reference software units (btld, flsl, swfk, swfl) to be assigned to this PDX-component-container.
These referenced software-units have already been successfully delivered to SWL-Cockpit with a
previous PDX-component-container and are already available there.
Further Information: can be found in the instructions
ESys_Handlungsanweisung_partieller_KC.pdf.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -pdxcontainer <PDX container definition file> -out <PDX container file> [
-uncompressedPDX] [-saveExtractedPDXFolder]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -pdxcontainer <PDX container definition file> -out <PDX container
file> [-uncompressedPDX] [-saveExtractedPDXFolder]
Declaration:
283
-pdxcontainer <PDX container definition file> Absolute path of the definition-file.
-out <PDX container file> Absolute path of the PDX-container to be
generated.
-uncompressedPDX Flag indicating whether the PDX file is generated
uncompressed. This might make the generation
faster but the PDX files will also be larger.
-saveExtractedPDXFolder Flag indicating where the extracted PDX will be
persisted after E-Sys is closed
Example:
E-Sys.bat -pdxcontainer C:\Data\pdx_def.xml -out C:\Data\ODX
\TEST__03__I020.001_023_020.pdx
Information:
• The PDX-container-definition-file describes the contents of the component-container. It is read
and a corresponding PDX-container is created and stored below the specified path.
• SWE files (BTLD, SWFL, SWFK, FLSL) of a specific ECU can be defined by reference only (see
SWEReferenceList). Such SWE are not part of the created container and are not present in the
container.
The software unites, that are listed under the reference (SWEReferenceList) are no real existing
software unit that will be at the container.
• A simple definition-file has the following content:
<PDXContainerDefinition xmlns="http://bmw.com/2010/esys.data.pdxcontainerdefinition">
  <PDXTemplate>C:/Data/ODX/F001_template.002_006_009.pdx</PDXTemplate>
  <BRVList>
  <BRV>F001</BRV>
  <BRV>F010</BRV>
  </BRVList>
  <ECUVariantList>
  <ECUVariant name="ECU1">
  <BaseVariant>EVALBOARD</BaseVariant>
  <SWEList> <!--List of software unites, that are part of the
container (existing at the container)-->
  <File>C:/Data/SWE/btld_01020304_002_000_000.bsw</File>
  </SWEList>
  <SWEReferenceList> <!--List of software unites that are no part
of the container (the hash value reference only to an at swl-cockpit already existing
software) -->
  <TE checksum="735208badabcd1e447c217f30aa621b0"
descTableStartAddress ="1">btld_01234567_004_005_006</TE>
  <TE checksum="d8462a1b22db2c88b29bc6dc989b2004"
descTableStartAddress ="13FE44">swfl_01234567_007_005_001</TE>
  </SWEReferenceList>
284
  </ECUVariant>
  </ECUVariantList>
</PDXContainerDefinition>
• With the optional entry <PDXDeterministic> set to true deterministic flash files will be
generated, otherwise the flash files will be generated with a non-deterministic ID’s.
• The XML-file is defined by the PDXContainerDefinition.xsd schema (see <E-SysInstallationsverzeichnis>/help). The schema defines all elements and describes them in more
detail in comentaries that can be used in the definition file.
As in the command-line, all paths of files and directories must be absolute in the definition-file.
• If errors occur, an error-file (named errors… txt) will be create. It is placed in the directory
where the PDX-container is stored and contains the error messages of the errors that occurred.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Creation of containers using Smart Actuators (SMAC)
Containers can consist of ECUs, SMACs or a combination of these. For usage of SMACs, the container
definition XML file makes use of the SMACVariant XML tag (under SMACVariantList). SMACs do not
use base variants. The name of a SMAC must be according to the EE component name which is
connected to the BTLD used in its SWEList.
See full example:
<PDXContainerDefinition xmlns="http://bmw.com/2010/esys.data.pdxcontainerdefinition">
  <PDXTemplate>C:\Data\PT01_template.003_100_000.pdx</PDXTemplate>
  <BRVList>
  <BRV>S15C</BRV>
  <BRV>S18A</BRV>
  </BRVList>
  <ECUVariantList>
  <ECUVariant name="NEU_EV">
  <BaseVariant>BDC_GW3</BaseVariant>
  <SWEList>
<File>C:\data\SWE\btld_00004139.bsw.008_041_040</File>
  </SWEList>
  </ECUVariant>
  </ECUVariantList>
  <SMACVariantList>
  <SMACVariant name="SMAC-TEST01">
  <SWEList>
<File>C:\Data\SWE\btld_0000ac0b.bsw.011_000_001</File>
285
  </SWEList>
  </SMACVariant>
  </SMACVariantList>
</PDXContainerDefinition>
Notice:
The command to create a container with SMACs remains as for a KC with ECUs. Only the content of
the definition file must be adapted.
Merge multiple PDX-Container
This command can be used to package multiple component-containers into one componentcontainer.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -mergepdxcontainer <PDX container definition file> -out <PDX container file>
[-uncompressedPDX] [-saveExtractedPDXFolder]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -mergepdxcontainer <PDX container definition file> -out <PDX
container file> [-uncompressedPDX] [-saveExtractedPDXFolder]
Declaration:
-mergepdxcontainer <PDX container definition
file>
Absolute path of the definition-file.
-out <PDX container file> Absolute path of the PDX-container to be
generated.
-uncompressedPDX Flag indicating whether the PDX file is generated
uncompressed. This might make the generation
faster but the PDX files will also be larger.
-saveExtractedPDXFolder Flag indicating where the extracted PDX will be
persisted after E-Sys is closed
Example:
E-Sys.bat -mergepdxcontainer C:\Data\pdx_merge.xml -out C:\Data\ODX
\TEST__03__I020.001_023_020.pdx
Information:
• The PDX-container-definition-file describes the contents of the component-container. The file
286
contains the path, the template to use for the component-container (element <PDXTemplate>), and
the paths of the to merge 
PDX-containers (element <ContainerList>). The file is read and a corresponding PDX-container is
created, which is stored below the path specified on the command-line
• A simple definition-file has the following content:
<PDXContainerDefinitionMerge
xmlns="http://bmw.com/2010/esys.data.pdxcontainerdefinition">
  <PDXTemplate>C:/Data/ODX/F001_template.002_006_009.pdx</PDXTemplate>
  <ContainerList>
  <File>C:/Data/ODX/F001_EKPM__03.001.000.001.pdx</File>
  <File>C:/Data/ODX/F001_DME__MSD85.001.001.002.pdx</File>
  <File>C:/Data/ODX/F001_EGS__GKEB23.002.008.003.pdx</File>
  </ContainerList>
</PDXContainerDefinitionMerge>
• The XML-file is defined by the PDXContainerDefinition.xsd schema (see <E-SysInstallationsverzeichnis>/help). The schema defines all elements and contains additional detail
in the form of comments which can be used in the definition file.
• As in the command-line, all path directories must be absolute in the definition-file.
• If errors occur, an error-file (named errors… txt) will be create. It is placed in the directory
where the PDX-container is stored and contains the error messages of the errors that occurred.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• Not supported:
◦ ECU-Variant-Patterns
◦ Documentation files of component containers
◦ Merging containers with the same ECU variants
PDX component containers name convention
Component containers should be created according to the following name convention:
<E/E Component>__<freetext>.<version>.pdx
E/E Component [A-Z0-9_]\{1,8}__[A-Z0-9_]\{1,8} E.g., ZBE__04
Free text [A-Z0-9_]\{1,20} E.g., F001
Version \d{3}_\d{3}_\d{3} E.g., 003_004_000
Example of a valid component container name: ZBE04F001.003_004_000.pdx
287
Each version part must be in in the range [0-255]. Any other value will not be allowed. For example,
ZBE04F001.003_004_256.pdx is an invalid component container name.
20.13. Proxy
If an active proxy has been defined in the properties (proxy.useProxy=true), it is taken into account
in both client- and server-client-based E-Sys-batch calls, 
even if you did not use a -setProxy in the server-client-batch.
If the proxy-server requires authentication (proxy.authRequired=true in the Properties), you are
prompted to enter the login and password for the proxy.
Only Basic-authentication is currently supported as an authentication method on the proxy server.
Legend:
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
Read Proxy-Status
The current Proxy-Status is output to stdout.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readStatusProxy
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readStatusProxy
Declaration:
-readStatusProxy command.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -readStatusProxy
Information:
• Here is an example edition:
A proxy is used:
288
https://web-proxy.de:8080
Noproxy-authenticationrequired
Do not use proxy on the following URLs:
https://bmw.de
https://bmwgroup.com
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred, so no verification was possible.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Setting a Proxy
The command provides the required proxy information: (proxy-host, proxy-port, proxyauthentication, username, password, URL-blacklist) E-Sys.
An active proxy is considered for all backend calls.
Command in client batch mode:
---Only applicable in server-client operation---
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -setProxy <configuration file> [-dialog]
Declaration:
-setProxy <config file> Absolute path to the configuration-file with the
proxy-server-parameters.
-dialog Backend-Login with GUI-dialog.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -server -setProxy c:\data\proxyConfig.config
E-Sys.bat -server -setProxy c:\data\proxyConfig.config -dialog
Information:
• If the switch -dialog is defined, a GUI-dialog is displayed in which authentication-data must be
entered.
• The authentication-dialog looks like this: .Authentication dialog
289
• The format of the configuration-file to pass is defined as follows:
# Proxy-URL e.g.: https://web-proxy.de
PROXY_HOST = <URL>
# Proxy-Port z.B. 8080
PROXY_PORT = <Port>
# Proxy authentication required
# DEFAULT = off
PROXY_AUTH = <on|off>
# PROXY_USERNAME is mandatory parameter if PROXY_AUTH = on
PROXY_USERNAME = <Proxy ID>
# PROXY_EXCLUDE_LIST is an optional parameter, but if it is used, the file must be in
the file path
# A list of the backend-URLs for which an active proxy should not be used.
PROXY_EXCLUDE_LIST = <file-path to the list>
• The command is only supported in server-client-mode.
• Necessary parameters are PROXY_HOST and PROXY_PORT.
• Optional parameters are PROXY_AUTH, PROXY_USERNAME, and PROXY_EXCLUDE_LIST. If
omitted, the information from the E-Sys.properties-file is read or default settings are used.
• The set proxy-settings are stored in the properties (except PROXY_USERNAME).
• The value of the PROXY_USERNAME is used only for the course of the E-Sys-session. There is no
Proxy-ID storage.
• If PROXY_AUTH = set on, the password for proxy must be entered manually in the commandline of the E-Sys-server.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred, so no verification was possible.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
290
Turn off Proxy
Do not use a set Proxy anymore.
Command in client batch mode:
---Only applicable in server-client operation---
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -removeProxy
Declaration:
-removeProxy command.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -server -removeProxy
Information:
• The command is only supported in server-client-mode.
• In the Config-file, the use of Proxy is disabled, all other proxy settings remain.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred, so no verification was possible.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.

SWT-Action
This command can be used to perform an SWT action.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -swtaction <config file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -swtaction <config file>
293
Declaration:
-swtaction <config file> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -swtaction C:\conf\connection.properties
Information:
• The concrete SWT-action is defined in the configuration-file together with the Connection
parameter and the following parameters:
FA = <FA-Filename>
VIN = <VIN-String>
# write_vin|store|update|upgrade|deactivate
SWT_ACTION = <SWT Aktion>
BASE_VARIANT = <Basevariant>
DIAG_ADDRESS = <Diagnoseadress (hex)>
APPLICATION_NUMBER = <Applikationsnumber>
UPGRADE_INDEX = <Upgrade-Index>
FSC = <FSC-Filename>
• No concurrent indication of FA and VIN is allowed.
• The FSC is only necessary for the store and upgrade actions.
• For the write_vin action, the VIN parameter must be defined.
• The write_vin action does not take into account the parameters APPLICATION_NUMBER and
UPGRADE_INDEX.
• The store\|update\|upgrade\|deactivate actions must always have the parameters
BASE_VARIANT, DIAG_ADDRESS, APPLICATION_NUMBER, and UPGRADE_INDEX defined.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
20.15. TAL processing
Legend:
294
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
With this batch-mode you can program and encode ECUs (SWE and CAF).
Before you can start a TAL-processing in the batch, you must first import the appropriate container.
You can import PDX containers using the instructions described at PDX Containers.
Note: Programming protection; mirror protocol and their impact on TAL processing.
TAL-processing
This command starts a TAL-processing.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -talexecution <config file> [-ignoreBATHAF]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -talexecution <config file> [-ignoreBATHAF]
Declaration:
-talexecution <config file> Absolute path to configuration file.
-ignoreBATHAF Optional parameter. Ignores the S1-switch.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -talexecution C:\conf\connection.properties -ignoreBATHAF
Information:
• If a BAT/HAF test reveals that switch S1 is open, the further execution of the command depends
on parameter -ignoreBATHAF.
◦ -ignoreBATHAF has been set: The flash sequence continues. However, the user must be aware
that the execution can lead to interruptions. In this case, the TAL-processing cannot be
ended with value 0 (OK), but at best with value 4 (with warning).
◦ -ignoreBATHAF not set: The execution of the command -talexecution is canceled.
• In the configuration file, the following parameters can be defined in addition to the Connection
parameter.
295
TAL = <TAL-Filename>
FA = <FA-Filename>
VIN = <VIN-String>
SVT = <SVT-Filename>
# fa|shipment|ncd (Default: fa)
CODING_TYPE = <Coding-Type>
# optional path indication where the NCDs are located
# Format <NCD-path 1>;<NCD-path 2>... , e.g.
"C:/NCD/00001234_0000dddd.caf.026_000_002.ncd;C:/NCD/00012345_0000bbbb.caf.006_011_008
.ncd"
# Only considered for coding type "ncd". Caution: only one ECU may be handled during
NCD encoding.
NCD_LIST = <NCD-path 1>;
# Perform FA-coding locally
# on|off OR true|false
USE_LOCAL_NCD = on
# Optional path where the NCDs are located, attention: in this directory a subfolder
with the VIN as the name is searched.
# If omitted, the NCD directory is used, which is specified in the settings. (stored
in properties)
# Only considered for coding type "fa" und "shipment".
PATH_NCD = C:/signedNCD/
# on|off
PARALLEL_PROGRAMMING = off
# on|off
CHECK_PROGRAMMING_COUNTER = on
# off|all|progress|transaction|error|tal|aep
EVENT= <Event-Filter for console output>
# on|off
FILL_INSTALLED_ECU_LIST = on
# merge|overwrite
FILL_INSTALLED_ECU_LIST_MODE = <Mode, how to fill the InstalledECUList>
# on|off
MODE_SWITCH_PROGRAMMING = <Mode-Switch during programming on/off>
# List of ECUs (diagnostic addresses in HEX), to be switched to programming mode.
# Without the parameter, all available ECUs are switched.
# E.g.: 10,63
296
ECUS_TO_SWITCH_TO_PROGRAMMING_MODE = <Ecu List>
# Absolute path to TAL-Filter-file.
TAL_FILTER = <TAL-Filter-Filename>
# Absolute path to a backup-directory with Individual-data.
IDR_BACKUP_PATH = <IDR-Backup-Directory>
# on|off (If the parameter is on, the mileage is read out before the TAL-processing
and writtenin fingerprint.)
READ_MILEAGE_FROM_GWSZ = off
# Mileage for Fingerprint
# If a valid value is specified, this will be written in Fingerprint, independent of
the mileage being read out.
# Default value '0' is used for Fingerprint, if neither MILEAGE nor
READ_MILEAGE_FROM_GWSZ was indicated
MILEAGE = <0-655330>
# URL of HDD-Update Servers
HDD_UPDATE_SERVER_URL = <URL for HDD-Update>
# on|off (Response on event during TAL-processing enable/disable)
ROE_DEACTIVATION = off
# on|off (prevent Http-transmission-protocol during TAL-processing)
PREVENT_HTTP_TRANSMISSION = off
# on|off (perform Optimized Bootloader flash on ECUs that support this functionality.
OPTIMIZABLE_BOOTLOADER_FLASH = off
# on|off (check expectedSgbmids)
EXPECTED_SGBMID_VALIDATION = on
# Optional Parameter.
# If specified, only client-batch-mode is considered
# Default value = off
USE_SWL_SEC_CERTIFICATE = <on|off>
# Optional Parameter.
# Default value = on
# Filters through MDR SGBM IDs
FILTER_MDR_SGBMIDS = <on|off>
# Optional Parameter.
# Default value = off
# Enable flashing of delta SWEs
ENABLE_DELTA_SWE_FLASH = <on|off>
# Optional Parameter. Considered only in client-batch-mode.
# If the parameter is omitted SWL_SEC_CONNECTION, the value from Esys.properties is
297
used.
SWL_SEC_CONNECTION = <bmw_intranet|internet>
# Optional Parameter.
# Specify whether all SWEn for SMAC should always be transmitted.
# If deactivated, only required SWEn are transferred. SWEn that are already present
and valid on the smart actuator are skipped.
FORCE_SWE_TRANSMISSION_FOR_SMAC_SWES = <on|off>
# Optional Parameter.
# List of ECUs (diagnostic addresses in HEX) for which no UDS fallback may be
performed.
# Alternatively, 'all' can be specified to disable the UDS fallback for all ECUs.
# The enumerated diagnostic addresses are only separated by a comma. No space may be
inserted between the enumeration of the diagnostic addresses!
# Without the parameter, the UDS flash is executed in case of an HTTP error.
# E.g.: 10,63
ECUS_TO_PREVENT_UDS_FALLBACK = < Diagnosis adresses in HEX> | all >
# Optional Parameter.
# UseCase Programming Protection BASIC (Field Mode)
# If not set and a token is required for programming protection basic, the token is
automatically requested in the SFA backend.
PROGRAMMING_PROTECTION_BASIC_TOKEN = <absolute path to signed token (json)>
# Optional Parameter.
# UseCase Programming Protection PLUS (Plant Mode)
PROGRAMMING_PROTECTION_PLUS_TOKEN = <absolute path to signed token file (JSON)>
# Optional Parameter.
# UseCase Mirror-Protocol
# Possible values: WITHOUT_AUTH, SIGNED_TOKEN, PLANT_TOKEN, SFA_TOKEN
# Default value = WITHOUT_AUTH
AUTH_METHOD_MIRROR_PROTOCOL = <WITHOUT_AUTH | SIGNED_TOKEN | PLANT_TOKEN | SFA_TOKEN>
# Optional Parameter.
# Mirror-Protocol UseCases: Authentication methods SIGNED_TOKEN, PLANT_TOKEN,
SFA_TOKEN
# Mandatory for authentication methods SIGNED_TOKEN, PLANT_TOKEN, SFA_TOKEN
UNSIGNED_TOKEN_FOR_MIRROR_PROTOCOL = <absolute path to unsigned token file>
# Optional Parameter.
# Mirror-Protocol UseCase: Authentication method SIGNED_TOKEN
# Mandatory for authentication method SIGNED_TOKEN
# This token is created by signing the unsigned token specified in the
UNSIGNED_TOKEN_FOR_MIRROR_PROTOCOL parameter (should only be used for SP21 ECUs)
# The unsigned token is generated using the unsignedTokenCreation command, and must be
created before TAL execution
# So that the signed token can be used during TAL execution
SIGNED_TOKEN_FOR_MIRROR_PROTOCOL = <absolute path to signed token file>
298
# Optional Parameter, for EES25 ECUs or newer
# Mirror-Protocol UseCase: Authentication method SFA-TOKEN offline
# If the parameter is not set, the token is requested in SFA backend (online BMWIntranet)
PROGRAMMING_PROTECTION_TOKEN = <absolute path to SFA token file>
# Optional Parameter, for EES25 ECUs or newer
# Mirror-Protocol UseCase: Authentication method PLANT-TOKEN offline
# If the parameter is not set, the token is requested in SFA backend (online BMWIntranet)
PLANT_MODE_TOKEN = <absolute path to PLANT-Mode token file>
• Because of "safe coding", a connection to the SWL-Sec2 must be established before executing a
TAL with coding elements. This also means that the computer must have two NICs. Since E-Sys
potentially has two different connections active at the same time (SWL-Sec2 backend and
vehicle).
• Communication with the SFA backend is required for processing a TAL with mirror protocol or
program protection-relevant transactions.
• A TAL with coding elements can only be run in E-Sys without server-client operation if:
◦ a Backend authentication for Coding[client Certificate for SWL Security System] is imported
and the parameter USE_SWL_SEC_CERTIFICATE is active
◦ OR the required test-keys are available locally
◦ OR the parameter USE_LOCAL_NCD is active (NCDs are signed locally)
◦ OR at CODING_TYPE=ncd (NCDs are signed locally)
• Necessary parameters are TAL, PROJECT, VEHICLEINFO and FA or VIN.
• The configuration file can contain either an FA or a VIN, but not both. If an FA is specified, it
must contain a VIN.
• An FA is mandatory to handle a TAL with coding-actions (coding-TAs). Applies to
CODING_TYPE=fa or shipment.
• CODING_TYPE = ncd allows you to encode an SG with an already existing NCD file. The option
NCD_LIST is absolutely necessary.
• With CODING_TYPE = ncd, only one ECU may be encoded during a TAL-processing.
• If the configuration-file contains the parameter HDD_UPDATE_SERVER_URL, an HDD-update is
performed, otherwise a TAL-processing is performed.
• For the switches PARALLEL_PROGRAMMING, CHECK_PROGRAMMING_COUNTER and
FILL_INSTALLED_ECU_LIST the values "on" and "off" can be defined.
• The default value for the parameters is the GUI values (from the Esys.properties file).
• A '\' may not be used in the configuration file. Instead, use '/' or '\\' for path [.underline]
Information:.
• The path information: for the parameters TAL, FA and TAL_FILTER can be both, absolute and
relative. For relative path information:, the reference point is the location of the config-file.
299
• All other E-Sys settings are read from the Esys.Properties file.
• The history of the TAL-processing is stored in the E-Sys log file.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 2 - The action was performed with errors.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Check Programming Protection
This command can be used to output which components are subject to authorization for the
current flash operation.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -isTokenForSecureFlashRequired -connection <config> -tal <path>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -isTokenForSecureFlashRequired -connection <config> -tal <path>
Information:
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file.
-tal Absolute path to TAL
Example:
E-Sys.bat -isTokenForSecureFlashRequired -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
-tal C:\Data\TAL.xml
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Generate Unsigned Token
A signed Programming Token is required to execute a TAL with Mirror-Depoy actions. Therefore a
file with Unsigned programming Tokens needs to be created.
300
This command can be used to generate an Unsigned Programming Token file.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -unsignedTokenCreation <config file path>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -unsignedTokenCreation <config file path>
Information:
-unsignedTokenCreation <config file path> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -unsignedTokenCreation C:\conf\configFile
Information:
In the configuration file, the following parameters (beside others) need to be defined in addition to
the Connection parameter:
TAL=<TAL-Filename>
VIN=<VIN-String>
SVT_SOLL=<SVT_Target-Filename>
UNSIGNED_TOKEN_FOR_MIRROR_PROTOCOL=<absolute path to unsigned token file>
• If successful the command will create a Unsigned Programming Token File at the specified path.
20.16. TAL calculation
A TAL is calculated from an SVT-actual- and an SVT-target-file.
Legend:
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
TAL-calculation
This command calculates a TAL
301
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -talcalculation <config file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -talcalculation <config file>
Declaration:
-talcalculation <config file> Absolute path to configuration file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -talcalculation C:\conf\connection.properties
Information:
In the configuration-file, the following parameters can be defined in addition to the Connection
parameter:
#Absolute path of the SVT-Actualfile
SVT_IST=<SVT-Actual-file>
#Absolute path of the SVT-Targetfile
SVT_SOLL=<SVT-Target-file>
#Absolute path of the generated TAL file
GENERATED_TAL=<TAL-filename>
#Absolute path to a TAL-Filter file.
TAL_FILTER=<TAL-Filter-filename>
#normal|idrBackup|idrRestore
TAL_TYPE=<TAL-Type>
#Absolute path to a Backup - Directory with Individual-data.
IDR_BACKUP_PATH=<IDR-Backup-Directory>
# on\|off
USE_MIRROR_PROTOKOLL=<mirror-protocol-usage>
• Required parameters are SVT-Actual, SVT-Target, and GENERATED_TAL.
• In standalone mode, additional connection parameters are required (see Connection
parameter)
302
• In server-client-mode, the server must have a PSdZ-connection open.
• The default value for the parameters is the GUI values (from the Esys.properties file).
• A '\' may not be used in the configuration file. Instead, use '/' or '\\' for path
• If the parameter TAL_TYPE has the value idrRestore, the parameter IDR_BACKUP_PATH must
also be defined.
• By default the value defined in the property TalGeneration.param.useMirror (from the
Esys.properties file) sets the USE_MIRROR_PROTOKOLL. However, if the parameter
USE_MIRROR_PROTOKOLL is defined, it will override the value previously defined. If none of
these properties are defined, the default value will be false.
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The action was successful.
◦ 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Example TAL Filter:
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<talfilter>
  <allEcu>
  <blUpdate>empty</blUpdate>
  <cdDeploy>empty</cdDeploy>
  <fscDeploy>empty</fscDeploy>
  <hwDeinstall>empty</hwDeinstall>
  <hwInstall>empty</hwInstall>
  <idBackup>empty</idBackup>
  <idDelete>empty</idDelete>
  <idRestore>empty</idRestore>
  <swDeploy>empty</swDeploy>
  <ibaDeploy>empty</ibaDeploy>
  <hddUpdate>empty</hddUpdate>
  <gatewayTableDeploy>empty</gatewayTableDeploy>
  </allEcu>
  <ecuFilter>
  <!-- decimal diagnostic address -->
  <diagAdr>10</diagAdr>
  <setting>
  <blUpdate>mustBeTreated</blUpdate>
  <cdDeploy>mustNotBeTreated</cdDeploy>
  <fscDeploy>mustNotBeTreated</fscDeploy>
  <hwDeinstall>allowedToBeTreated</hwDeinstall>
  <hwInstall>mustNotBeTreated</hwInstall>
  <idBackup>mustNotBeTreated</idBackup>
  <idDelete>mustNotBeTreated</idDelete>
  <idRestore>mustNotBeTreated</idRestore>
  <swDeploy>mustNotBeTreated</swDeploy>
303
  <ibaDeploy>mustNotBeTreated</ibaDeploy>
  <hddUpdate>mustNotBeTreated</hddUpdate>
  <gatewayTableDeploy>mustNotBeTreated</gatewayTableDeploy>
  </setting>
  </ecuFilter>
</talfilter>

The following data can be read and written from the VCM (VCM-Master or VCM-Backup): FA, FP,
SVT-Target, I-Step, VIN.
305
Write VCM-Master (FA, I-Step or SVT-Target)
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -writeVcmMaster <FA|ISTUFEN|SVTSOLL> -connection <config file> -in <source
file>
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -writeVcmMaster <FA|ISTUFEN|SVTSOLL> [-connection <config file>] -in
<source file>
Declaration:
-writeVcmMaster <FA|ISTUFEN|SVTSOLL> Parameters that can take the value FA, ISTUFEN
or SVTSOLL.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-in <source file> Absolute path for "FA-file", "text file with I-step"
or "SVT-Target-file".
Example:
E-Sys.bat -writeVcmMaster FA -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -in C:\Data\F
A\FA_Y120BX.xml
E-Sys.bat -writeVcmMaster ISTUFEN -in C:\Data\istufen_Y120BX.txt
E-Sys.bat -writeVcmMaster SVTSOLL -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -in C:
\Data\SVT\SVT_SOLL_Y120BX.xml
Information:
• The I-Steps are to be passed in the "Text-file with I-Steps" in the following format:
<CurrentI-Step>
<LastI-Step>
<Auslieferungs-I-Step>
• The I-Steps are specified in the usual format, e.g. S15A-15-07-500
• The following codes are returned:
◦ 0 - The processing was completed successfully.
306
◦ 1 - Errors have occurred.
◦ 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
◦ 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.

parameter).

\FA_123.xml

P\FP_123.xml

\Data\SVT\SVTSOLL_123.xml

FA_Master_<VIN>_<Timestamp>.xml is located in the destination directory.
• FP: If no file name is specified, the selected FP with the following file name:
FP_Master_<VIN>_<Timestamp>.xml is located in the destination directory.
• I-Stufe: If no file name is specified, the destination directory contains the i-levels read with the
following file name: ISTUFEN_Master_<VIN>_<Timestamp>.txt
• SVT-Target: If no file name is specified, the selected SVTSOLL with the following file name:
