20.19. Certificate Management
For Certificate Management, batch offers the following commands.
Legend:
315
• [] optional, can be specified, but does not have to
• () selection, must be specified
• | "or", is used in a selection
Read Certificate
With the following batch command, it is possible to read from the ECUs according to the container
type provided.
 Attention! Not all ECUs support reading of all container types.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readCERT -connection <config file> -type <Certificate type> [-svt <SVT
file>] [-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readCERT -connection <config file> -type <Certificate type> [-svt
<SVT file>] [-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Declaration:
-readCERT command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-type <Certificate type> Type of Certificate to read: CERTIFICATE,
BINDING, ONLINE_CERTIFICATES_ECU or
SEC_OC_KEYLIST.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -readCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -type CERTIFICATE
-blacklist C:\Daten\blacklist.txt
E-Sys.bat -readCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -type BINDING -svt C:
\SVT\SVT_I20.xml -whitelist C:\Daten\whitelist.txt
E-Sys.bat -readCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -type
ONLINE_CERTIFICATES_ECU -svt C:\SVT\SVT_I20.xml -blacklist C:\Daten\blacklist.txt
316
-whitelist C:\Daten\whitelist.txt
E-Sys.bat -readCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -type SEC_OC_KEYLIST
Information:
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Generating a Certificate request
This command generates a request file to the CBB. This can then be passed on to the corresponding
process (web interface, mail).
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -generateCSR -connection <config file> -out <target file> [-noSecOCKeys] [
-vin <VIN17>]
[-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -generateCSR -connection <config file> -out <target file> [
-noSecOCKeys] [-vin
<VIN17>] [-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Declaration:
-generateCSR command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-out <target file> Absolute path to the target file.
-noSecOCKeys Disable Restbus Keys. Do not add a virtual ECU
to the CBB request file.
-vin <VIN17> 17-digit VIN.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.
317
Example:
E-Sys.bat -generateCSR -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -out C:\Data\CERT
\requestCBB[JSON].txt
Information:
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Send a Certificate request to the CBB and save the response (online)
This command sends a request file to the CBB. The obtained result is stored in a CBB response file.
This command can only be used in the BMW environment, as Certificates are obtained from
one/more servers.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -getCbbResponseFromRequest <cbb request file> [-out <target directory>] (
-connection <config file> | -svt <SVT file>)
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -getCbbResponseFromRequest <cbb request file> [-out <target
directory>] (-connection <config file> | -svt <SVT file>)
Declaration:
-getCbbResponseFromRequest <cbb request file> Absolute path to CBB-Request-file.
-out <target directory> Absolute path to the target file. If omitted, the
default path is used for CBB response files.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT file.
Example:
318
E-Sys.bat -getCbbResponseFromRequest C:\Data\CERT\WBAAE810X0H123456_CBBRequest.txt
-out C:\cert\cert.txt -svt C:\svt.xml
E-Sys.bat -getCbbResponseFromRequest C:\Data\CERT\WBAAE810X0H123456_CBBRequest.txt
-out C:\cert\cert.txt -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
Information:
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
Writing the bindings from file
This command writes all bindings, Certificates, and bindings from the specified response file from
the CBB to the connected vehicle. The "Other Bindings" are also generated and also written into the
vehicle.
The -secOCKeys option also displays a file for residual bus simulation.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -writeBindings -connection <config file> -in <CBB response file> [
-noSecOCKeys] [-svt <SVT file>] [-secOCKeysPath <SecOCKeyPack file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -writeBindings -connection <config file> -in <CBB response file> [
-noSecOCKeys] [-svt <SVT file>] [-secOCKeysPath <SecOCKeyPack file>]
Declaration:
-writeBindings command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-in <CBB response file> Absolute path to file.
-noSecOCKeys Disable Restbus Keys. Do not add a virtual ECU
to the CBB request file.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
319
-secOCKeysPath <SecOCKeyPack file> Absolute path to the target file with symmetric
keys. Only considered without the secOCKeys
parameter.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -writeBindings -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -in
C:\Daten\WBAAE810X0H123456_CBBResponse_20210331_125817[JSON].txt" -secOCKeysPath C:
\Data\CERT\Keys\20210102_131515_SecOC_KeyPack_plain.xml
Information:
If the parameter -secOCKeysPath SecOCKeyPack target file is omitted, the default path is used.
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Checking the Certificates on the Certificate-enabled ECUs
This command can be used to initiate a Certificate check in the ECU. After the internal inspection is
complete, E-Sys waits for the longest returned inspection time of the ECUs. After that, the results are
requested and written to result files. The status is read out in parallel for several ECUs, taking into
account the topology.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -checkCERT -connection <config file> -retries <value> [-svt <SVT file>] [
-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -checkCERT -connection <config file> -retries <value> [-svt <SVT
file>] [-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Declaration:
-checkCERT command.
320
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-retries <value> Number of performed scans (for 1 to a
maximum of 10). example: -retries 5).
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to SVT-file.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -checkCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -retries 3
E-Sys.bat -checkCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -retries 3 -blacklist
C:\Daten\blacklist.txt
E-Sys.bat -checkCERT -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -retries 3 -blacklist
C:\Daten\blacklist.txt -whitelist C:\Daten\whitelist.txt
Information:
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
Checking the persistent certificates stored in the certificate-enable ECUs
This command performs a check of persistently stored certificates and keys, if available.
The results are displayed in the console and written to a file.
Two types of checks can be performed:
• Quick: a fast/quick check
• Full: a complete check of certificates, including the certificate signatures
By default, a quick check is performed. To perform a complete check, the option -full should be
used.
Command in client batch mode:
321
E-Sys.bat -checkPersistentCert [-full] -connection <config file> [-retries <value>] [
-svt <SVT file>] [-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -checkPersistentCert [-full] -connection <config file> [-retries
<value>] [-svt <SVT file>] [-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Declaration:
-checkPersistentCert command.
-full To perform a complete check of certificates.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-retries <value> Number of scans to perform (range: 1 to 10). If
not specified a default value (i.e., 1) will be used.
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to the SVT file.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to the blacklist file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to the whitelist file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -checkPersistentCert -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
E-Sys.bat -checkPersistentCert -full -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
E-Sys.bat -checkPersistentCert -full -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
-retries 3 -blacklist C:\Data\blacklist.txt
E-Sys.bat -checkPersistentCert -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -retries 3
-blacklist C:\Data\blacklist.txt -whitelist C:\Data\whitelist.txt
Information:
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.
322
Deleting the persistent certificates and keys stored in the certificate-enable
ECUs
This command deletes the following data from ECUs:
• every keypair of all individual certificates (only in the development phase, as long as they are
not already stored in the HSM / SHE)
• every generated CSR
• the signatures of all generated CSRs
• every installed individual certificate
• the timestamp of the individual certificates, so older certificate can be installed
• the generated keylist
• the signature of the generated keylist
• the timestamp of the keypack
• all symmetric SecOC keys
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -deleteCertKeys connection <config file> [-svt <SVT file>] [-blacklist
<file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -deleteCertKeys connection <config file> [-svt <SVT file>] [
-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>]
Declaration:
-deleteCertKeys command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-svt <SVT file> Absolute path to the SVT file.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to the blacklist file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to the whitelist file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -deleteCertKeys -connection C:\conf\connection.properties
E-Sys.bat -deleteCertKeys -connection C:\conf\connection.properties

ata\blacklist.txt

ata\blacklist.txt -whitelist C:\Data\whitelist.txt

• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.

Setting the Freshness Value of a specific SecOC ECU
This command can be used to write a new SecOC Counter value to the ECU. The affected ECUs must
be in Engineering-Mode.
Either the black/white mechanism may be used as a parameter (blacklist and/or whitelist) or
diagaddress.
If neither diagnostic address nor blacklist/whitelist is passed, the new SecOc Counter value is set for
all SecOc-enabled ECUs.
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -setSecOCCounter -connection <config file> -value <hex value> \{ [
-diagaddress <diagnosis address>] \| \{[-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>] } }
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -setSecOCCounter -connection <config file> -value <hex value> \{ [
-diagaddress <diagnosis address>] \| \{[-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>] } }
Declaration:
-setSecOCCounter command.
-connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the
connection parameter (see Connection
parameter).
-value <hex value> Counter-Value as HEX in range of 0x0 to
0xFFFFFFFF.
-diagaddress <diagnosis address> The diagnostic address of the ECU.
-blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file.
-whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.
Example:
E-Sys.bat -setSecOCCounter -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -value 0x01
-diagaddress 0x33
E-Sys.bat -setSecOCCounter -connection C:\conf\connection.properties -value 0x01
328
-blacklist C:\Daten\blacklist.txt -whitelist C:\Daten\whitelist.txt
Information:
The following codes are returned:
• 0 - The action was successful.
• 1 - An exception occurred so the action could not be completed.
• 2 - The action was performed with errors.
• 3 - Unable to connect to the server.
• 4 - The action was performed without errors but with warnings.

Example:

external_WBA45678901234568_20231002071339.crt


which it applies, should be present on the <certificate file> file name. This file
should also include the certificate chain with CA and subCA.
Example: service-29-PENTEST_OIDC_User-PW_without_proof_of_possesionWBA11412412425235.json
That will expectedly be the case for certificates obtained at Sec4Diag backend.
See also Print E-Sys public key.

20.19.2. Read SecOC State
This command reads the SecOC state of all target ECUs. In this context, SecOC state means:
• SecOC status
• Keypack status
• Keypack creation time status
• LCS1 current status
• Response status
• ECU unknown status
Command in client batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -readSecOCState -connection <config file> { [-diagaddress
<diagnosis address>] | {[-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>] } }
Command in client-server batch mode:
E-Sys.bat -server -readSecOCState -connection <config file> { [-diagaddress
<diagnosis address>] | {[-blacklist <file>] [-whitelist <file>] } }
Declaration:
• -readSecOCState command.
• -connection <config file> Absolute path to configuration file with the connection parameter
• -diagaddress <diagnosis address> The diagnostic address of the ECU.
• -blacklist <file> Absolute path to Blacklist-file.
• -whitelist <file> Absolute path to Whitelist-file.
20.20. Connection parameter
In order to establish a connection, the following parameters can be defined in a batch configuration
file:
PROJECT = <project name>
VEHICLEINFO = <vehicle info>
# bus|gateway_url|icom_d_can|icom_ethernet|icom_vcpi|vin
CONNECTION = <connection type>
 The specification of the PROJECT parameter is mandatory, but this specification is
343
not evaluated. For the connection establishment the project specification is
determined by the name of the imported containers. This information is
determined from the ECU-Config files.
The parameter Connection is optional. Without this parameter the information’s are read from file
E-Sys.properties. If the parameter is defined, the batch configuration file has to consist the
following parameter depending on the connection type:
Connection type bus:
# z.B. BODY_CAN, FLEXRAY, SYSTEMBUS_ETHERNET, A_CAN, D_CAN, ...
BUS_NAME = <bus name>
# VECTOR_DIRECT | VECTOR_DIRECT_FLEXRAY | PASS_THRU | MEDIA_CONVERTER
INTERFACE = <interface>
# If BUS_NAME=SYSTEMBUS_ETHERNET and INTERFACE=MEDIA_CONVERTER, it is necessary to set
the parameter URL
# Format <protocoll>://<IP address>:<port>
URL = <URL matching the format above>
Connection type gateway_url, icom_d_can, icom_ethernet, icom_vcpi:
# Format <protocoll>://<IP address>:<port>
URL = <URL matching the format above>
Connection type vin:
GATEWAY_VIN = AUTODETECT
If this option is used, E-Sys will search for all possible VINs to establish a connection. Then, if:
• VINs = 1 - The VIN is used to establish a connection
• VINs = 0 - No connection will be established, because no VINs were found
• VINs > 1 - No connection will be established, because multiple VINs were found
GATEWAY_VIN = AUTODETECT_DIAGADR<gateway diagnostic address hex> (e.g.,
AUTODETECT_DIAGADR0010)
If this option is used, E-Sys will search for all possible VINs to establish a connection. Then, if there
is a VIN for the specified diagnostic address, E-Sys will try to establish this connection. If there are
multiple VINs for the given diagnostic address or none, the connection process will be aborted.
The following vehicle-specific parameters should be defined:
344
# on|off
READ_VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER
# used if READ_VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER = off
VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER_SERIES = <series>
# used if READ_VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER = off
VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER_ISTEP_SHIPMENT = <I-step>
For the value on of parameter READ_VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER, the series and I-step will be read
from VCM.
Otherwise, the parameters VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER_SERIES and
VEHICLE_CONNECTION_PARAMETER_ISTEP_SHIPMENT will be read. If any of these parameters are left
undefined, a warning message will be written to the log file. Despite the warning, the connection
will attempt to be established.
Secure diagnostics
EES25 introduces the concept of secure diagnostics. A secure diagnostics connection requires tester
authentication on the vehicle gateway, using a Service29 certificate. To provide support for this use
case, the following connection parameter has been introduced:
# on|off
# - on: a secure diagnostic session will be established with the vehicle
# - off (or absence of property in the connection file): an unsecure diagnostic
session will be
# establish with the vehicle
CONNECTION_WITH_AUTHENTICATION = on

In order to successfully establish a connection with authentication, the user must
have a Service29 certificate, matching the VIN of the vehicle, imported beforehand
into E-Sys keystore.
See Add Service29 certificate.
345
E-Sys | (c) BMW Group, powered by Critical TechWorks
